%matplotlib inline

from tensorflow.keras.models import Sequential

def encode_text_dummy(df, name):
    dummies = pd.get_dummies(df[name])
    for x in dummies.columns:
        dummy_name = "{}-{}".format(name, x)
        df[dummy_name] = dummies[x]
    df.drop(name, axis=1, inplace=True)

# Convert all missing values in the specified column to the median
def missing_median(df, name):
    med = df[name].median()
    df[name] = df[name].fillna(med)

def encode_numeric_range(df, name, normalized_low=-1, normalized_high=1,
                         data_low=None, data_high=None):
    if data_low is None:
        data_low = min(df[name])
        data_high = max(df[name])

    df[name] = ((df[name] - data_low) / (data_high - data_low)) \
               * (normalized_high - normalized_low) + normalized_low
    
def encode_text_index(df, name):
    le = preprocessing.LabelEncoder()
    df[name] = le.fit_transform(df[name])
    return le.classes_

def to_xy(df, target):
    result = []
    for x in df.columns:
        if x != target:
            result.append(x)
    # find out the type of the target column. 
    target_type = df[target].dtypes
    target_type = target_type[0] if isinstance(target_type, Sequence) else target_type
    # Encode to int for classification, float otherwise. TensorFlow likes 32 bits.
    if target_type in (np.int64, np.int32):
        # Classification
        dummies = pd.get_dummies(df[target])
        return df[result].values.astype(np.float32), dummies.values.astype(np.float32)
    else:
        # Regression
        return df[result].values.astype(np.float32), df[target].values.astype(np.float32)


def encode_numeric_zscore(df, name, mean=None, sd=None):
    if mean is None:
        mean = df[name].mean()

    if sd is None:
        sd = df[name].std()

    df[name] = (df[name] - mean) / sd
def plot_confusion_matrix(cm, names, title='Confusion matrix', cmap=plt.cm.Blues):
    plt.imshow(cm, interpolation='nearest', cmap=cmap)
    plt.title(title)
    plt.colorbar()
    tick_marks = np.arange(len(names))
    plt.xticks(tick_marks, names, rotation=45)
    plt.yticks(tick_marks, names)
    plt.tight_layout()
    plt.ylabel('True label')
    plt.xlabel('Predicted label')
    
def report_coef(names,coef):
    r = pd.DataFrame( { 'coef': coef, 'positive': coef>=0  }, index = names )
    r = r.sort_values(by=['coef'])
    display(r)
    r['coef'].plot(kind='barh', color=r['positive'].map({True: 'b', False: 'r'}))

Pre Regularization FNN Model¶

Pre Regularization FNN Trial 1

In [147]:
checkpointer = ModelCheckpoint(filepath="dnn/best_weights.hdf5", verbose=0, save_best_only=True)
for i in range(2):
    print(i)

    model = Sequential()
    model.add(Dense(5, input_dim=x.shape[1], activation='sigmoid'))
    model.add(Dense(5))
    model.add(Dense(2, activation='softmax'))

    adam = optimizers.Adam(lr=0.01, beta_1=0.9, beta_2=0.999, epsilon=None, decay=0.0, amsgrad=False)
    sgd = optimizers.SGD(lr=.001)
    model.compile(loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', optimizer=sgd)

    monitor = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=1e-3, patience=5, verbose=1, mode='auto')
    

    model.fit(x_train,y_train,validation_data=(x_test,y_test), batch_size= 32, callbacks=[monitor,checkpointer],verbose=2,epochs=500)

    
model.load_weights('dnn/best_weights.hdf5') 


pred = model.predict(x_test)
pred = np.argmax(pred,axis=1)
#y_true = np.argmax(y_test,axis=1)

score = metrics.accuracy_score(y_test, pred)
print("Final accuracy: {}".format(score))

Pre Regularization FNN Trial 2

In [20]:
checkpointer = ModelCheckpoint(filepath="dnn/best_weights.hdf5", verbose=0, save_best_only=True)
for i in range(2):
    print(i)

    model = Sequential()
    model.add(Dense(5, input_dim=x.shape[1], activation='tanh'))
    model.add(Dense(5))
    model.add(Dense(2, activation='softmax'))

    adam = optimizers.Adam(lr=0.01, beta_1=0.9, beta_2=0.999, epsilon=None, decay=0.0, amsgrad=False)
    sgd = optimizers.SGD(lr=.001)
    model.compile(loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', optimizer=sgd)

    monitor = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=1e-3, patience=5, verbose=1, mode='auto')
    

    model.fit(x_train,y_train,validation_data=(x_test,y_test), batch_size= 32, callbacks=[monitor,checkpointer],verbose=2,epochs=500)

    
model.load_weights('dnn/best_weights.hdf5') 


pred = model.predict(x_test)
pred = np.argmax(pred,axis=1)
#y_true = np.argmax(y_test,axis=1)

score = metrics.accuracy_score(y_test, pred)
print("Final accuracy: {}".format(score))

Pre Regularization FNN Trial 3

In [21]:
checkpointer = ModelCheckpoint(filepath="dnn/best_weights.hdf5", verbose=0, save_best_only=True)
for i in range(2):
    print(i)

    model = Sequential()
    model.add(Dense(5, input_dim=x.shape[1], activation='tanh'))
    model.add(Dense(5))
    model.add(Dense(2, activation='softmax'))

    adam = optimizers.Adam(lr=0.01, beta_1=0.9, beta_2=0.999, epsilon=None, decay=0.0, amsgrad=False)
    sgd = optimizers.SGD(lr=.001)
    model.compile(loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', optimizer=sgd)

    monitor = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=1e-3, patience=5, verbose=1, mode='auto')
    

    model.fit(x_train,y_train,validation_data=(x_test,y_test), batch_size= 32, callbacks=[monitor,checkpointer],verbose=2,epochs=500)

    
model.load_weights('dnn/best_weights.hdf5') 


pred = model.predict(x_test)
pred = np.argmax(pred,axis=1)
#y_true = np.argmax(y_test,axis=1)

score = metrics.accuracy_score(y_test, pred)
print("Final accuracy: {}".format(score))

Pre Regularization FNN Trial 4

In [23]:
checkpointer = ModelCheckpoint(filepath="dnn/best_weights.hdf5", verbose=0, save_best_only=True)
for i in range(2):
    print(i)

    model = Sequential()
    model.add(Dense(5, input_dim=x.shape[1], activation='sigmoid'))
    model.add(Dense(5))
    model.add(Dense(2, activation='softmax'))

    adam = optimizers.Adam(lr=0.01, beta_1=0.9, beta_2=0.999, epsilon=None, decay=0.0, amsgrad=False)
    sgd = optimizers.SGD(lr=1e-6)
    model.compile(loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', optimizer=adam)

    monitor = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=1e-3, patience=5, verbose=1, mode='auto')
    

    model.fit(x_train,y_train,validation_data=(x_test,y_test), batch_size= 32, callbacks=[monitor,checkpointer],verbose=2,epochs=500)

    
model.load_weights('dnn/best_weights.hdf5') 


pred = model.predict(x_test)
pred = np.argmax(pred,axis=1)
#y_true = np.argmax(y_test,axis=1)

score = metrics.accuracy_score(y_test, pred)
print("Final accuracy: {}".format(score))

checkpointer = ModelCheckpoint(filepath="dnn/best_weights.hdf5", verbose=0, save_best_only=True)
for i in range(2):
    print(i)

    model = Sequential()
    model.add(Dense(5, input_dim=x.shape[1], activation='sigmoid'))
    model.add(Dense(5))
    model.add(Dense(2, activation='softmax'))

    adam = optimizers.Adam(lr=0.0001, beta_1=0.9, beta_2=0.999, epsilon=None, decay=0.0, amsgrad=False)
    sgd = optimizers.SGD(lr=1e-6)
    model.compile(loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', optimizer=adam)

    monitor = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=1e-3, patience=5, verbose=1, mode='auto')
    

    model.fit(x_train,y_train,validation_data=(x_test,y_test), batch_size= 32, callbacks=[monitor,checkpointer],verbose=2,epochs=500)

    
model.load_weights('dnn/best_weights.hdf5') 


pred = model.predict(x_test)
pred = np.argmax(pred,axis=1)
#y_true = np.argmax(y_test,axis=1)

score = metrics.accuracy_score(y_test, pred)
print("Final accuracy: {}".format(score))

In [179]:
checkpointer = ModelCheckpoint(filepath="dnn/best_weights.hdf5", verbose=0, save_best_only=True)
for i in range(2):
    print(i)

    model = Sequential()
    model.add(Dense(5, input_dim=x.shape[1], activation='tanh'))
    model.add(Dense(5))
    model.add(Dense(2, activation='softmax'))

    adam = optimizers.Adam(lr=0.01, beta_1=0.9, beta_2=0.999, epsilon=None, decay=0.0, amsgrad=False)
    sgd = optimizers.SGD(lr=1e-6)
    model.compile(loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', optimizer=adam)

    monitor = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=1e-3, patience=5, verbose=1, mode='auto')
    

    model.fit(x_train,y_train,validation_data=(x_test,y_test), batch_size= 32, callbacks=[monitor,checkpointer],verbose=2,epochs=500)

    
model.load_weights('dnn/best_weights.hdf5') 


pred = model.predict(x_test)
pred = np.argmax(pred,axis=1)
#y_true = np.argmax(y_test,axis=1)

score = metrics.accuracy_score(y_test, pred)
print("Final accuracy: {}".format(score))

Pre Regularization CNN Model Trial 1

In [42]:
cnn = Sequential()
cnn.add(Conv2D(256, kernel_size=(1, 2), strides=(1, 1),
                 activation='sigmoid',
                 input_shape=(1, 13, 1)))


cnn.add(MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(1,2)))

cnn.add(Conv2D(256, kernel_size=(1, 2), strides=(1, 1),
                 activation='tanh'))
cnn.add(MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(1,2)))
    
    
cnn.add(Flatten())
cnn.add(Dense(1024, activation="sigmoid"))
cnn.add(Dropout(0.5))
cnn.add(Dense(2, activation="softmax"))

# define optimizer and objective, compile cnn

cnn.compile(loss="sparse_categorical_crossentropy", optimizer="sgd")

x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(xx, y, test_size=0.2, random_state=42)

import time

start_time = time.time()
checkpointer = ModelCheckpoint(filepath="dnn/best_weights.hdf5", verbose=0, save_best_only=True)
for i in range(5):
    print(i)

    monitor = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=1e-3, patience=5, verbose=1, mode='auto')
    cnn.fit(x_train[0:15000], y_train[0:15000],     
              batch_size=64,
              epochs=10,
              verbose=2,
               callbacks=[monitor,checkpointer],
              validation_data=(x_test[0:300], y_test[0:300]))

pred2 = cnn.predict(x_test)
pred2 = np.argmax(pred2,axis=1)
#y_true = np.argmax(y_test,axis=1)

score = metrics.accuracy_score(y_test, pred2)
print("Final accuracy: {}".format(score))

cnn = Sequential()
cnn.add(Conv2D(256, kernel_size=(1, 2), strides=(1, 1),
                 activation='relu',
                 input_shape=(1, 13, 1)))


cnn.add(MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(1,2)))

cnn.add(Conv2D(256, kernel_size=(1, 2), strides=(1, 1),
                 activation='relu'))
cnn.add(MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(1,2)))
    
    
cnn.add(Flatten())
cnn.add(Dense(1024, activation="sigmoid"))
cnn.add(Dropout(0.5))
cnn.add(Dense(2, activation="softmax"))

# define optimizer and objective, compile cnn

cnn.compile(loss="sparse_categorical_crossentropy", optimizer="adam")

x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(xx, y, test_size=0.2, random_state=42)

import time

start_time = time.time()
checkpointer = ModelCheckpoint(filepath="dnn/best_weights.hdf5", verbose=0, save_best_only=True)
for i in range(5):
    print(i)

    monitor = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=1e-3, patience=5, verbose=1, mode='auto')
    cnn.fit(x_train[0:2000], y_train[0:2000],     
              batch_size=64,
              epochs=10,
              verbose=2,
               callbacks=[monitor,checkpointer],
              validation_data=(x_test[0:300], y_test[0:300]))

pred2 = cnn.predict(x_test)
pred2 = np.argmax(pred2,axis=1)
#y_true = np.argmax(y_test,axis=1)

score = metrics.accuracy_score(y_test, pred2)
print("Final accuracy: {}".format(score))

FNN Trials After Regularization¶

In [214]:
x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(x, y, test_size=0.2, random_state=42)

FNN Post Regularization Trial 1

In [215]:
checkpointer = ModelCheckpoint(filepath="dnn/best_weights.hdf5", verbose=0, save_best_only=True)
for i in range(2):
    print(i)

    model = Sequential()
    model.add(Dense(10, input_dim=x.shape[1], activation='relu'))
    model.add(Dense(10))
    model.add(Dense(10))
    model.add(Dense(2, activation='softmax'))

    adam = optimizers.Adam(lr=0.01, beta_1=0.9, beta_2=0.999, epsilon=None, decay=0.0, amsgrad=False)
    sgd = optimizers.SGD(lr=1e-6)
    model.compile(loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', optimizer=adam)

    monitor = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=1e-3, patience=5, verbose=1, mode='auto')
    

    model.fit(x_train,y_train,validation_data=(x_test,y_test), batch_size= 32, callbacks=[monitor,checkpointer],verbose=2,epochs=500)

    
model.load_weights('dnn/best_weights.hdf5') 


pred = model.predict(x_test)
pred = np.argmax(pred,axis=1)
#y_true = np.argmax(y_test,axis=1)

score = metrics.accuracy_score(y_test, pred)
print("Final accuracy: {}".format(score))

In [109]:
checkpointer = ModelCheckpoint(filepath="dnn/best_weights.hdf5", verbose=0, save_best_only=True)
for i in range(2):
    print(i)

    model = Sequential()
    model.add(Dense(5, input_dim=x.shape[1], activation='tanh'))
    model.add(Dense(5))
    model.add(Dense(2, activation='softmax'))

    adam = optimizers.Adam(lr=0.01, beta_1=0.9, beta_2=0.999, epsilon=None, decay=0.0, amsgrad=False)
    sgd = optimizers.SGD(lr=1e-6)
    model.compile(loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', optimizer=sgd)

    monitor = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=1e-3, patience=5, verbose=1, mode='auto')
    

    model.fit(x_train,y_train,validation_data=(x_test,y_test), batch_size= 32, callbacks=[monitor,checkpointer],verbose=2,epochs=500)

    
model.load_weights('dnn/best_weights.hdf5') 


pred = model.predict(x_test)
pred = np.argmax(pred,axis=1)
#y_true = np.argmax(y_test,axis=1)

score = metrics.accuracy_score(y_test, pred)
print("Final accuracy: {}".format(score))

FNN Post Regularization Trial 4

In [110]:
checkpointer = ModelCheckpoint(filepath="dnn/best_weights.hdf5", verbose=0, save_best_only=True)
for i in range(2):
    print(i)

    model = Sequential()
    model.add(Dense(5, input_dim=x.shape[1], activation='relu'))
    model.add(Dense(5))
    model.add(Dense(2, activation='softmax'))

    adam = optimizers.Adam(lr=0.01, beta_1=0.9, beta_2=0.999, epsilon=None, decay=0.0, amsgrad=False)
    sgd = optimizers.SGD(lr=.001)
    model.compile(loss='sparse_categorical_crossentropy', optimizer=sgd)

    monitor = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=1e-3, patience=5, verbose=1, mode='auto')
    

    model.fit(x_train,y_train,validation_data=(x_test,y_test), batch_size= 32, callbacks=[monitor,checkpointer],verbose=2,epochs=500)

    
model.load_weights('dnn/best_weights.hdf5') 


pred = model.predict(x_test)
pred = np.argmax(pred,axis=1)
#y_true = np.argmax(y_test,axis=1)

score = metrics.accuracy_score(y_test, pred)
print("Final accuracy: {}".format(score))

CNN Trials After Regularization¶

CNN Post Regularization Trial 1

In [153]:
xx= x.reshape((4500,1,13,1))
In [154]:
cnn = Sequential()
cnn.add(Conv2D(256, kernel_size=(1, 2), strides=(1, 1),
                 activation='relu',
                 input_shape=(1, 13, 1)))


cnn.add(MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(1,2)))

cnn.add(Conv2D(256, kernel_size=(1, 2), strides=(1, 1),
                 activation='relu'))
cnn.add(MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(1,2)))
    
    
cnn.add(Flatten())
cnn.add(Dense(1024, activation="sigmoid"))
cnn.add(Dropout(0.5))
cnn.add(Dense(2, activation="softmax"))

# define optimizer and objective, compile cnn

cnn.compile(loss="sparse_categorical_crossentropy", optimizer="adam")

x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(xx, y, test_size=0.2, random_state=42)

import time

start_time = time.time()
checkpointer = ModelCheckpoint(filepath="dnn/best_weights.hdf5", verbose=0, save_best_only=True)
for i in range(5):
    print(i)

    monitor = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=1e-3, patience=5, verbose=1, mode='auto')
    cnn.fit(x_train[0:2000], y_train[0:2000],     
              batch_size=64,
              epochs=10,
              verbose=2,
               callbacks=[monitor,checkpointer],
              validation_data=(x_test[0:300], y_test[0:300]))

pred2 = cnn.predict(x_test)
pred2 = np.argmax(pred2,axis=1)
#y_true = np.argmax(y_test,axis=1)

score = metrics.accuracy_score(y_test, pred2)
print("Final accuracy: {}".format(score))

cnn = Sequential()
cnn.add(Conv2D(256, kernel_size=(1, 2), strides=(1, 1),
                 activation='tanh',
                 input_shape=(1, 13, 1)))


cnn.add(MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(1,2)))

cnn.add(Conv2D(256, kernel_size=(1, 2), strides=(1, 1),
                 activation='tanh'))
cnn.add(MaxPooling2D(pool_size=(1,2)))
    
    
cnn.add(Flatten())
cnn.add(Dense(1024, activation="tanh"))
cnn.add(Dropout(0.5))
cnn.add(Dense(2, activation="softmax"))

# define optimizer and objective, compile cnn

cnn.compile(loss="sparse_categorical_crossentropy", optimizer="adam")

x_train, x_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(xx, y, test_size=0.2, random_state=42)

import time

start_time = time.time()
checkpointer = ModelCheckpoint(filepath="dnn/best_weights.hdf5", verbose=0, save_best_only=True)
for i in range(5):
    print(i)

    monitor = EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=1e-3, patience=5, verbose=1, mode='auto')
    cnn.fit(x_train[0:2000], y_train[0:2000],     
              batch_size=64,
              epochs=10,
              verbose=2,
               callbacks=[monitor,checkpointer],
              validation_data=(x_test[0:300], y_test[0:300]))

pred2 = cnn.predict(x_test)

#y_true = np.argmax(y_test,axis=1)
